    WHERE [p].[ID] = @__Parse_0
) AS [t]

    SELECT [p0].[ProductImagesFilesID], [p0].[ProductsID], [t1].[ID], [t1].[CreatedDate], [t1].[Discriminator], [t1].[FileName], [t1].[Path], [t1].[StorageType]
